## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: nonlinear oscillator dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models the acceleration of a nonlinear harmonic oscillator, where dv_dt depends on position x, velocity v, and possibly time t. Classical nonlinear oscillator equations (Duffing, van der Pol, Rayleigh, driven/damped systems) provide the relevant formula structures.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Linear restoring force: dv_dt = c0 * x (simple harmonic oscillator)
- Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (cubic nonlinear restoring force)
- Damped linear oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (linear damping with linear restoring force)
- Damped Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (cubic restoring + linear damping)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * x**2 * v (nonlinear damping depending on amplitude)
- Rayleigh oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (velocity-dependent nonlinear damping)
- Quintic nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 (higher-order restoring force)
- Driven oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * sin(c3 * t) (periodic external forcing)
- Parametric oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x * cos(c1 * t) (time-modulated stiffness)
- Nonlinear damping + Duffing: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * x**2 * v (combined van der Pol-Duffing)
- Coulomb-like friction: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v * (c2 + c3 * v**2) (velocity-dependent friction model)
- Softening/hardening spring: dv_dt = c0 * x * (1 + c1 * x**2) (amplitude-dependent effective stiffness)
- General polynomial: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 + c2 * x**3 + c3 * v (asymmetric restoring force with damping)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope ŌåÆ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects ŌåÆ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay ŌåÆ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior ŌåÆ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects ŌåÆ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Odd-power restoring forces (x, x**3, x**5) ŌåÆ symmetric potential wells preserving oscillator symmetry
- Even-power terms in x (x**2) ŌåÆ asymmetric potential, indicating broken spatial symmetry
- Velocity-position coupling terms like x**2*v ŌåÆ amplitude-dependent damping (van der Pol type nonlinearity)
- Cubic velocity terms v**3 ŌåÆ nonlinear dissipation (Rayleigh-type friction)
- Explicit sinusoidal time dependence sin(c*t) ŌåÆ externally driven/forced oscillator
- Product x*cos(c*t) ŌåÆ parametric excitation where stiffness is modulated in time
- Absence of explicit time dependence ŌåÆ autonomous system, energy conservation or limit cycle behavior
- Linear v term with negative coefficient ŌåÆ energy injection (self-excited oscillation) vs positive ŌåÆ dissipation

This has `log(c7*exp(c8*v) + 1)`. Let me check if this can equal `log(|v| + 1)`.

`log(c7*exp(c8*v) + 1)` is a softplus-type function. For this to equal `log(|v| + 1)`, we'd need `c7*exp(c8*v) + 1 = K*(|v| + 1)` for some constant K, which is impossible since exp is not equal to |v| for all v.

So Candidate 49 cannot match either. The softplus function `log(a*exp(bv)+1)` is smooth and analytic everywhere, while `log(|v|+1)` has a kink at v=0. These are fundamentally different functions.

- **Candidate 19**: Has `sin(c7*t + c8)` ŌĆö not log. NO MATCH.

**Conclusion:** None of the candidates contain a `log(|v| + ...)` term or any structure that could reproduce the logarithmic dependence on v present in the GT. All candidates are either polynomial or contain exp/sin terms that cannot replicate a logarithm.
